    12	impl<F: AcirField + DebugToString, Registers: RegisterAllocator> BrilligContext<F, Registers> {
    13	    /// Copy arguments to [ScratchSpace] and call [ProcedureId::VectorPopFront].
    14	    ///
    15	    /// Pops items from the front of a vector, returning the new vector.
    16	    /// The procedure assumes that there are constraints to prevent 0 size vectors from being popped.
    17	    pub(crate) fn call_vector_pop_front_procedure(
    18	        &mut self,
    19	        source_len: SingleAddrVariable,
    20	        source_vector: BrilligVector,
    21	        destination_vector: BrilligVector,
    22	        item_pop_count: usize,
    23	    ) {
    24	        let [
    25	            source_vector_length_arg,
    26	            source_vector_pointer_arg,
    27	            item_pop_count_arg,
    28	            destination_vector_pointer_return,
    29	        ] = self.make_scratch_registers();
    30	
    31	        self.mov_instruction(source_vector_length_arg, source_len.address);
    32	        self.mov_instruction(source_vector_pointer_arg, source_vector.pointer);
    33	        self.usize_const_instruction(item_pop_count_arg, item_pop_count.into());
    34	
    35	        self.add_procedure_call_instruction(ProcedureId::VectorPopFront);
    36	
    37	        self.mov_instruction(destination_vector.pointer, destination_vector_pointer_return);
    38	    }
    39	}
    40	
    41	/// Compile [ProcedureId::VectorPopFront].
    42	pub(super) fn compile_vector_pop_front_procedure<F: AcirField + DebugToString>(
    43	    brillig_context: &mut BrilligContext<F, ScratchSpace>,
    44	) {
    45	    let [
    46	        source_vector_length_arg,
    47	        source_vector_pointer_arg,
    48	        item_pop_count_arg,
    49	        destination_vector_pointer_return,
    50	    ] = brillig_context.allocate_scratch_registers();
    51	
    52	    let source_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: source_vector_pointer_arg };
    53	    let target_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: destination_vector_pointer_return };
    54	
    55	    let VectorMetaData {
    56	        rc: source_rc,
    57	        size: source_size,
    58	        capacity: source_capacity,
    59	        items_pointer: source_items_pointer,
    60	    } = brillig_context.codegen_read_vector_metadata(
    61	        source_vector,
    62	        Some((source_vector_length_arg, item_pop_count_arg)),
    63	    );
    64	
    65	    // target_size = source_size - item_pop_count
    66	    // Assumes constraints exist against underflow.
    67	    // We don't have to worry about the semantic length of merged vectors here, because we are popping from the front.
    68	    let target_size = brillig_context.allocate_single_addr_usize();
    69	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
    70	        source_size.address,
    71	        item_pop_count_arg,
    72	        target_size.address,
    73	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
    74	    );
    75	
    76	    let is_rc_one = brillig_context.codegen_usize_equals_one(*source_rc);
    77	
    78	    brillig_context.codegen_branch(is_rc_one.address, |brillig_context, is_rc_one| {
    79	        if is_rc_one {
    80	            // We reuse the source vector, moving the metadata to the right (decreasing capacity)
    81	            // Set the target vector pointer to be the source plus the number of popped items.
    82	            brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
    83	                source_vector.pointer,
    84	                item_pop_count_arg,
    85	                target_vector.pointer,
    86	                BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
    87	            );
    88	            // Decrease the source capacity by the number of popped items.
    89	            // This is done at the original address; it will be copied in the next step.
    90	            brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
    91	                source_capacity.address,
    92	                item_pop_count_arg,
    93	                source_capacity.address,
    94	                BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
    95	            );
    96	            // Re-initialize the metadata at the shifted position.
    97	            brillig_context.codegen_initialize_vector_metadata(
    98	                target_vector,
    99	                *target_size,
   100	                *source_capacity,
   101	            );
   102	        } else {
   103	            // We can't reuse the source vector, so allocate a new one.
   104	            brillig_context.codegen_initialize_vector(target_vector, *target_size, None);
   105	
   106	            let target_vector_items_pointer =
   107	                brillig_context.codegen_make_vector_items_pointer(target_vector);
   108	
   109	            // Set the source pointer to copy from to the source items start plus the number of popped items.
   110	            let source_copy_pointer = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   111	            brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   112	                source_items_pointer.address,
   113	                item_pop_count_arg,
   114	                *source_copy_pointer,
   115	                BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   116	            );
   117	            // Now we copy the source vector into the target vector, starting at index after the popped items.
   118	            brillig_context.codegen_mem_copy(
   119	                *source_copy_pointer,
   120	                *target_vector_items_pointer,
   121	                *target_size,
   122	            );
   123	            // We don't decrease the RC of the source vector, otherwise repeatedly popping the same item
   124	            // from the original (immutable) handle would bring its RC down to 1.
   125	        }
   126	    });

     2	
     3	use super::ProcedureId;
     4	use crate::brillig::brillig_ir::{
     5	    BrilligBinaryOp, BrilligContext,
     6	    brillig_variable::{BrilligVector, SingleAddrVariable},
     7	    debug_show::DebugToString,

    10	
    11	impl<F: AcirField + DebugToString, Registers: RegisterAllocator> BrilligContext<F, Registers> {
    12	    /// Copy arguments to [ScratchSpace] and call [ProcedureId::VectorRemove].
    13	    ///
    14	    /// Removes `item_count` items from the `source_vector` at `index`, returning the new `destination_vector`.
    15	    /// Modifies the `source_vector` if the reference count is 1.
    16	    ///
    17	    /// The procedure assumes that we have constraints on the index being within the semantic length of the vector.
    18	    pub(crate) fn call_vector_remove_procedure(
    19	        &mut self,
    20	        source_vector: BrilligVector,
    21	        destination_vector: BrilligVector,
    22	        index: SingleAddrVariable,
    23	        item_count: usize,
    24	    ) {
    25	        let [
    26	            source_vector_pointer_arg,
    27	            index_arg,
    28	            item_count_arg,
    29	            destination_vector_pointer_return,
    30	        ] = self.make_scratch_registers();
    31	
    32	        self.mov_instruction(source_vector_pointer_arg, source_vector.pointer);
    33	        self.mov_instruction(index_arg, index.address);
    34	        self.usize_const_instruction(item_count_arg, item_count.into());
    35	
    36	        self.add_procedure_call_instruction(ProcedureId::VectorRemove);
    37	
    38	        self.mov_instruction(destination_vector.pointer, destination_vector_pointer_return);
    39	    }
    40	}
    41	
    42	/// Compile [ProcedureId::VectorRemove].
    43	pub(super) fn compile_vector_remove_procedure<F: AcirField + DebugToString>(
    44	    brillig_context: &mut BrilligContext<F, ScratchSpace>,
    45	) {
    46	    let [source_vector_pointer_arg, index_arg, item_count_arg, destination_vector_pointer_return] =
    47	        brillig_context.allocate_scratch_registers();
    48	
    49	    let source_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: source_vector_pointer_arg };
    50	    let target_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: destination_vector_pointer_return };
    51	    let index = SingleAddrVariable::new_usize(index_arg);
    52	
    53	    // Reallocate if necessary
    54	    let source_size = brillig_context.codegen_read_vector_size(source_vector);
    55	
    56	    // We don't have to worry about the semantic length of merged vectors here, because we are removing an item,
    57	    // rather than appending it, so it doesn't matter if the semantic length was shorter than the vector size.
    58	    let target_size = brillig_context.allocate_single_addr_usize();
    59	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
    60	        source_size.address,
    61	        item_count_arg,
    62	        target_size.address,
    63	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
    64	    );
    65	
    66	    let rc = brillig_context.codegen_read_vector_rc(source_vector);
    67	
    68	    let is_rc_one = brillig_context.codegen_usize_equals_one(*rc);
    69	
    70	    let source_vector_items_pointer =
    71	        brillig_context.codegen_make_vector_items_pointer(source_vector);
    72	
    73	    // The items pointer in either the source vector of a new one, depending on reuse.
    74	    let target_vector_items_pointer = brillig_context.allocate_register();
    75	
    76	    // Set up the target vector up to the index.
    77	    brillig_context.codegen_branch(is_rc_one.address, |brillig_context, is_rc_one| {
    78	        if is_rc_one {
    79	            // We can reuse the source vector: update its length and set the items pointer to be the source.
    80	            brillig_context.mov_instruction(target_vector.pointer, source_vector.pointer);
    81	            brillig_context.codegen_update_vector_size(target_vector, *target_size);
    82	            brillig_context
    83	                .codegen_vector_items_pointer(target_vector, *target_vector_items_pointer);
    84	        } else {
    85	            // We need to copy the vector; allocate a new one with the target size.
    86	            brillig_context.codegen_initialize_vector(target_vector, *target_size, None);
    87	
    88	            // Get the items pointer for the new vector.
    89	            brillig_context
    90	                .codegen_vector_items_pointer(target_vector, *target_vector_items_pointer);
    91	
    92	            // Copy the elements to the left of the index.
    93	            brillig_context.codegen_mem_copy(
    94	                *source_vector_items_pointer,
    95	                *target_vector_items_pointer,
    96	                index,
    97	            );
    98	
    99	            // We don't modify the RC of the original, otherwise removing items repeatedly
   100	            // from the original (immutable) handle could bring its RC down to 1.
   101	        }
   102	    });
   103	
   104	    // Compute the source pointer after the removed items: source_after = source + index + item_count.
   105	    let source_pointer_after_index = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   106	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   107	        *source_vector_items_pointer,
   108	        index.address,
   109	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   110	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   111	    );
   112	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   113	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   114	        item_count_arg,
   115	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   116	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   117	    );
   118	
   119	    // Compute the target pointer at the index: target_at = target + index
   120	    let target_pointer_at_index = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   121	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   122	        *target_vector_items_pointer,
   123	        index.address,
   124	        *target_pointer_at_index,
   125	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   126	    );
   127	
   128	    // Compute the number of elements to the right of the index: item_count_right = source_size - index - item_count.
   129	    let item_count_right = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   130	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   131	        source_size.address,
   132	        index.address,
   133	        *item_count_right,
   134	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
   135	    );
   136	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   137	        *item_count_right,
   138	        item_count_arg,
   139	        *item_count_right,
   140	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
   141	    );
   142	
   143	    // Copy the elements to the right of the index
   144	    brillig_context.codegen_mem_copy(
   145	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   146	        *target_pointer_at_index,
   147	        SingleAddrVariable::new_usize(*item_count_right),
   148	    );
   149	}

   150	    /// representing the removed items, then create a new vector with the same number of
   151	    /// items removed and subsequent items shifted to the left.
   152	    pub(crate) fn slice_remove_operation(
   153	        &mut self,
   154	        target_vector: BrilligVector,
   155	        source_vector: BrilligVector,
   156	        index: SingleAddrVariable,
   157	        removed_items: &[BrilligVariable],
   158	    ) {

   173	        );

   394	    pub(crate) fn codegen_read_vector_metadata(
   395	        &mut self,
   396	        vector: BrilligVector,
   397	        semantic_length_and_item_size: Option<(MemoryAddress, MemoryAddress)>,
   398	    ) -> VectorMetaData<Registers> {
   399	        let rc = self.allocate_single_addr_usize();
   400	        let size = self.allocate_single_addr_usize();
   401	        let capacity = self.allocate_single_addr_usize();
   402	        let items_pointer = self.allocate_single_addr_usize();
   403	
   404	        // Vector layout: [ref_count, size, capacity, items...]
   405	        self.load_instruction(rc.address, vector.pointer);
   406	        let read_pointer = self.allocate_register();
   407	        self.codegen_usize_op(
   408	            vector.pointer,
   409	            *read_pointer,
   410	            BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   411	            offsets::VECTOR_SIZE,
   412	        );
   413	        if let Some((length, item_size)) = semantic_length_and_item_size {
   414	            self.codegen_vector_flattened_size(size.address, length, item_size);
   415	        } else {
   416	            self.load_instruction(size.address, *read_pointer);
   417	        }
   418	        self.codegen_usize_op_in_place(
   419	            *read_pointer,
   420	            BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   421	            offsets::VECTOR_CAPACITY - offsets::VECTOR_SIZE,
   422	        );
   423	        self.load_instruction(capacity.address, *read_pointer);
   424	        self.codegen_usize_op(
   425	            *read_pointer,
   426	            items_pointer.address,
   427	            BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   428	            offsets::VECTOR_ITEMS - offsets::VECTOR_CAPACITY,
   429	        );
   430

    10	
    11	impl<F: AcirField + DebugToString, Registers: RegisterAllocator> BrilligContext<F, Registers> {
    12	    /// Copy arguments to [ScratchSpace] and call [ProcedureId::VectorRemove].
    13	    ///
    14	    /// Removes `item_count` items from the `source_vector` at `index`, returning the new `destination_vector`.
    15	    /// Modifies the `source_vector` if the reference count is 1.
    16	    ///
    17	    /// The procedure assumes that we have constraints on the index being within the semantic length of the vector.
    18	    pub(crate) fn call_vector_remove_procedure(
    19	        &mut self,
    20	        source_vector: BrilligVector,
    21	        destination_vector: BrilligVector,
    22	        index: SingleAddrVariable,
    23	        item_count: usize,
    24	    ) {
    25	        let [
    26	            source_vector_pointer_arg,
    27	            index_arg,
    28	            item_count_arg,
    29	            destination_vector_pointer_return,
    30	        ] = self.make_scratch_registers();
    31	
    32	        self.mov_instruction(source_vector_pointer_arg, source_vector.pointer);
    33	        self.mov_instruction(index_arg, index.address);
    34	        self.usize_const_instruction(item_count_arg, item_count.into());
    35	
    36	        self.add_procedure_call_instruction(ProcedureId::VectorRemove);
    37	
    38	        self.mov_instruction(destination_vector.pointer, destination_vector_pointer_return);
    39	    }
    40	}
    41	
    42	/// Compile [ProcedureId::VectorRemove].
    43	pub(super) fn compile_vector_remove_procedure<F: AcirField + DebugToString>(
    44	    brillig_context: &mut BrilligContext<F, ScratchSpace>,
    45	) {
    46	    let [source_vector_pointer_arg, index_arg, item_count_arg, destination_vector_pointer_return] =
    47	        brillig_context.allocate_scratch_registers();
    48	
    49	    let source_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: source_vector_pointer_arg };
    50	    let target_vector = BrilligVector { pointer: destination_vector_pointer_return };
    51	    let index = SingleAddrVariable::new_usize(index_arg);
    52	
    53	    // Reallocate if necessary
    54	    let source_size = brillig_context.codegen_read_vector_size(source_vector);
    55	
    56	    // We don't have to worry about the semantic length of merged vectors here, because we are removing an item,
    57	    // rather than appending it, so it doesn't matter if the semantic length was shorter than the vector size.
    58	    let target_size = brillig_context.allocate_single_addr_usize();
    59	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
    60	        source_size.address,
    61	        item_count_arg,
    62	        target_size.address,
    63	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
    64	    );
    65	
    66	    let rc = brillig_context.codegen_read_vector_rc(source_vector);
    67	
    68	    let is_rc_one = brillig_context.codegen_usize_equals_one(*rc);
    69	
    70	    let source_vector_items_pointer =
    71	        brillig_context.codegen_make_vector_items_pointer(source_vector);
    72	
    73	    // The items pointer in either the source vector of a new one, depending on reuse.
    74	    let target_vector_items_pointer = brillig_context.allocate_register();
    75	
    76	    // Set up the target vector up to the index.
    77	    brillig_context.codegen_branch(is_rc_one.address, |brillig_context, is_rc_one| {
    78	        if is_rc_one {
    79	            // We can reuse the source vector: update its length and set the items pointer to be the source.
    80	            brillig_context.mov_instruction(target_vector.pointer, source_vector.pointer);
    81	            brillig_context.codegen_update_vector_size(target_vector, *target_size);
    82	            brillig_context
    83	                .codegen_vector_items_pointer(target_vector, *target_vector_items_pointer);
    84	        } else {
    85	            // We need to copy the vector; allocate a new one with the target size.
    86	            brillig_context.codegen_initialize_vector(target_vector, *target_size, None);
    87	
    88	            // Get the items pointer for the new vector.
    89	            brillig_context
    90	                .codegen_vector_items_pointer(target_vector, *target_vector_items_pointer);
    91	
    92	            // Copy the elements to the left of the index.
    93	            brillig_context.codegen_mem_copy(
    94	                *source_vector_items_pointer,
    95	                *target_vector_items_pointer,
    96	                index,
    97	            );
    98	
    99	            // We don't modify the RC of the original, otherwise removing items repeatedly
   100	            // from the original (immutable) handle could bring its RC down to 1.
   101	        }
   102	    });
   103	
   104	    // Compute the source pointer after the removed items: source_after = source + index + item_count.
   105	    let source_pointer_after_index = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   106	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   107	        *source_vector_items_pointer,
   108	        index.address,
   109	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   110	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   111	    );
   112	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   113	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   114	        item_count_arg,
   115	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   116	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   117	    );
   118	
   119	    // Compute the target pointer at the index: target_at = target + index
   120	    let target_pointer_at_index = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   121	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   122	        *target_vector_items_pointer,
   123	        index.address,
   124	        *target_pointer_at_index,
   125	        BrilligBinaryOp::Add,
   126	    );
   127	
   128	    // Compute the number of elements to the right of the index: item_count_right = source_size - index - item_count.
   129	    let item_count_right = brillig_context.allocate_register();
   130	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   131	        source_size.address,
   132	        index.address,
   133	        *item_count_right,
   134	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
   135	    );
   136	    brillig_context.memory_op_instruction(
   137	        *item_count_right,
   138	        item_count_arg,
   139	        *item_count_right,
   140	        BrilligBinaryOp::Sub,
   141	    );
   142	
   143	    // Copy the elements to the right of the index
   144	    brillig_context.codegen_mem_copy(
   145	        *source_pointer_after_index,
   146	        *target_pointer_at_index,
   147	        SingleAddrVariable::new_usize(*item_count_right),
   148	    );
